[张展关注组通告：本联署活动将于2021年12月28日（张展被判刑入狱四年之日）截止](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/20211228.html)
------

<div>
<span><a name='more'></a></span><p><br /></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><b>8</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><b>月初家人与狱方及张展通话后通报：张展体重降到不到<span lang="EN-GB">40</span>公斤，患有严重的营养不良、肠胃病、浮肿。<span lang="EN-GB">10</span>月底家人视频通话后通报：张展体重更减轻、无力行走、无力抬头、毫无血色、命悬一线、病入膏肓、身形完全走样。张展病危消息传出后，已有多家国际人权机构、美国国务院、德国外交部、英国驻华大使馆、联合国人权高专办、多位联合国人权专家、欧盟、美国国会等纷纷发布声明，呼吁立即释放张展，要求中国当局给予她及时充分的医疗救治，让她见家属、律师。但迄今一个多月过去了，关于张展病情、绝食情况、监狱如何对待她的情况，无确切消息；张展的律师于十月中旬到监狱递交会见申请，无回复；于<span lang="EN-GB">11</span>月<span lang="EN-GB">24</span>日到监狱管理局交涉，不被接待；张展的家人于<span lang="EN-GB">11</span>月两次分别给监狱管理局和监狱递交保外就医申请，无回音，无进展。（参见附录“关注张展时间线备忘”）</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">感谢各位在张展危难之际为她发声的海内外朋友！敬请继续关注病危的张展和她家人、律师的处境！</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">“请不要绝望，只要还在努力。”（张展）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">--</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">《关于给予张展全面身体检查和紧急救治的呼吁书》</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">及联署名单第十版<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><b>（<span lang="EN-GB">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-GB">12</span>月<span lang="EN-GB">16</span>日<span lang="EN-GB">10:00 GMT </span>更新，共<span lang="EN-GB">1179</span>人）</b></span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p><b>&nbsp;</b></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">上海市司法局局长、上海市女子监狱监狱长：</b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">我们作为公民，作为张展的朋友，作为钦佩张展良知的人，一直在关注张展的身体状况，最近从网上看到张展的哥哥所写的保外就医申请书，得知张展身体已经命悬一线，我们非常忧虑。为防止悲剧的发生，我们认为有必要写一封信给您，表达我们共同的诉求：那就是对张展进行全面的身体检查，同时对其进行紧急救治。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展一直绝食，这不是我们这些关心张展的人愿意看到的局面，我们也曾通过不同渠道劝说张展停止绝食保重自己来日方长，但张展有自己的信仰和坚持，从辩护律师和家人会见后透露的信息，结合张展的性格看，在判决前张展绝食并非为了获得轻判的结果，判决后张展也不是为了获得保外就医或监外执行的结果。张展更为纯粹，她就是通过绝食单纯地表达对迫害的不服。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">假如张展真的有罪，哪怕她自己认为无罪而绝食，形销骨立生命垂危，从安定法秩序的角度，我们也不会附议对她保外就医或监外执行，也不会呼吁您给她全面身体检查和紧急救助。</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">但是，张展是无罪的。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展是一个逆行者，在很多人惶恐的逃离武汉时，她却只身去了武汉，这种勇气殊为难得，如果是在民族危亡时，像张展这样的人才能毁家纾难取义成仁，可以说张展这种人是一个民族最可宝贵的精神财富。张展在武汉时，大多数时间她只是静静地记录，记录武汉市民疫情下的生活，偶尔会帮助发一点求救信息，丝毫没有干扰政府的防疫救灾工作。她在疫情期间扮演的角色本质上就是一个公民记者，这样的行为怎么就寻衅滋事了？</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在大灾大难面前，哪怕政府的力量再强大，也需要公民做一些辅助性的工作，公民逆行去灾难现场，是一个现代政府应当鼓励的行为，不仅客观上有助于救灾，而且也在塑造一种互助友爱的社会氛围，后者可能更为宝贵。对张展这种完全无害只有助益的行为动用刑事手段进行惩罚，是不义的。</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">我们说张展的无罪，不仅是自然法意义上的无罪，也是实在法意义上的无罪。张展无害的行为根本没有社会危害性，也完全不符合寻衅滋事罪的犯罪构成。张展对迫害的不服从在法理情三方面都能站得住脚。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展作为一个虔诚的基督徒，她很谦卑的看待自己，在武汉期间的行为低调谦和不事张扬，将自己隐身于其中，没有什么世俗功利的想法。如果不是上海这样一个国际大都市的公检法对她抓捕、迫害，没有多少人知道她。这是个事实，说出这点无损于张展的形象，张展就像一颗埋在海沙里的珍珠，别人是否发现她识得她，她都仍然是一颗珍珠，她自己也毫不在意。</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展现在获得的国际国内的广泛关注都是拜上海有司滥权枉法所赐，今天张展身体命悬一线，如果真的发生了死亡的悲剧，这必将会有一场国际国内谴责控诉的狂飙，那时没有谁是赢家。张展的父母失去女儿，我们失去朋友，中国失去一个优秀的公民，而你们上海公检法司将会背负永恒的历史罪责。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展是一位你们从未见过的硬骨头，在她的字典里没有苟且这两个字，为了抗议对自己的迫害甚至不惜决志殉道，这是一个你们需要直面的现实，不要再拖延试图令她屈服，那只会进一步摧垮她的身体。我们迫切请求你们尽速给张展做全面的身体检查并给予紧急的救治，以免贻误救治的时机。</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">我们之所以要求在保外就医或者监外执行之前，给张展做一个全面的身体检查并给予紧急救治，是因为我们不仅认为她应当被释放，更应当健康的活下来，而不是像一些良心犯那样在弥留之际才获准保外就医，几天后死亡而让迫害者逃脱历史的罪责。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">我们的要求并不过分，因为张展本来就是无罪的，因为张展被抓捕前是健康的，而贵局负有保障被羁押者身体不至于垮掉的职责。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">公元二〇二一年十一月十二日</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color: #1b1b1b; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">署</span><span style="color: #1b1b1b; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名</span><span style="color: #1b1b1b; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">征集信箱：<span lang="EN-GB">shifangzhangzhan@gmail.com</span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">联署名单</span></b><b><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">：</span></b><span style="color: #1b1b1b; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">唐吉田，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">谢　阳，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">王　宇，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">王全璋，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">李大伟，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">马连顺，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">刘书庆，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: &quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;;"> </span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.5pt; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">要人扶着走路，说话时连头都无力扬着，再不保外就医，很危险！</span><span style="color: #050505; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: inherit, serif;">"</span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #050505; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-font-family: inherit; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">厘米，正常体重是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #050505; font-family: &quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;;">60-65</span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-font-family: inherit; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">公斤。自张展被关押至浦东看守所，到转押至女子监狱期间，因为种种原因，张展的身体羸弱不堪。我问医生，张展是否可能死去？医生明确回答我可能性很大。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #050505; font-family: &quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;;"> 2021</span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-font-family: inherit; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #050505; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;;">29</span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-font-family: inherit; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">日，我母亲得到监狱通知，去监狱和张展进行了视频会见。我母亲见到的张展，比我们在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #050505; font-family: &quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;;">8</span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-font-family: inherit; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">月份电话中听到的还要虚弱，张展的体重恐怕更加不足</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #050505; font-family: &quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;;">40</span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-font-family: inherit; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">公斤，走路需要人搀扶，脖子无力支撑脑袋，脸上和额头上皮包骨头、毫无血色，已经命悬一线。张展目前的身体状况不能独自走路。在搀扶和支撑下，勉强可以行走</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #050505; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-font-family: inherit; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">米的距离。我母亲闻此噩耗，万分悲痛，甚至向监狱工作人员双膝下跪，希望他们能给予张展人道的照顾。</span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: &quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;;"> </span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">的相关条件。</span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: &quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;;"> </span><span style="color: #050505; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-font-family: inherit; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Segoe UI Historic&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: inherit;">无论从相关法律规定或者人道主义原则出发，我们特此申请，请批准允许张展保外就医。我们深知，张展案件具有一定的敏感性。从家人的角度，我们愿意配合警察、监狱等相关部门的相关要求。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #050505; font-family: &quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;
